  <script type="text/javascript">
   //get temperature for DC from weather API
link = "https://api.openweathermap.org/data/2.5/weather?id=4140963&units=metric&appid=eba50a420452d1bc7b1c033682b3d41d";
var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
var gallaTemp;
request.open('GET',link,true);
request.onload = function(){
 var obj = JSON.parse(this.response);
 if (request.status >= 200 && request.status < 400) {
 gallaTemp = obj.main.temp;
 gallaTemp = Math.ceil(gallaTemp * (9/5) + 32);
 document.querySelector("#gallaTemp p").textContent = gallaTemp + "°";
 }
 else{
  console.log("The city doesn't exist! Kindly check");
 }
}
request.send();
  </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     (function( $, window, document, undefined ) {
				if( jQuery('.widgetopts-placeholder-e').length > 0 ){
					// jQuery('.elementor-column-wrap:has(.widgetopts-placeholder-e)').hide();
					jQuery('.elementor-section:has(.widgetopts-placeholder-e)').each( function(){
						var pTop 	= jQuery( this ).find('.elementor-element-populated').css('padding-top');
						var pBot 	= jQuery( this ).find('.elementor-element-populated').css('padding-bottom');
						var pHeight = jQuery( this ).find('.elementor-element-populated').innerHeight();
						var vert	= pHeight - ( parseFloat( pTop ) + parseFloat( pBot ) );
						
						if( typeof vert !== 'undefined' && vert < 5 ){
							jQuery( this ).hide();
						}else{
							jQuery( this ).find( '.widgetopts-placeholder-e' ).each(function(){
								jQuery( this ).closest( '.elementor-element' ).hide();
								
								var countEl 	= jQuery( this ).closest( '.elementor-column' ).find('.elementor-element').length;
								var countHolder = jQuery( this ).closest( '.elementor-column' ).find('.widgetopts-placeholder-e').length;
								if( countEl == countHolder ){
									jQuery( this ).closest( '.elementor-column' ).hide();
								}
							}).promise().done( function(){
								var sTop 	= jQuery( this ).closest('.elementor-section').css('padding-top');
								var sBot 	= jQuery( this ).closest('.elementor-section').css('padding-bottom');
								var sHeight = jQuery( this ).closest('.elementor-section').innerHeight();
								var svert	= sHeight - ( parseFloat( sTop ) + parseFloat( sBot ) );
								
								if( typeof svert !== 'undefined' && svert < 5 ){
									jQuery( this ).closest('.elementor-section').hide();
								}
							});
						}
					} );
				}
			})( jQuery, window, document );
    </script>

    <!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 9: Remove South Regionals 2021 + Update Midwest by Central -->
    <script>
     // Remove of the 2021 South Section:

var removeSouth2021 = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82490 li');
if (removeSouth2021 != null){ 
	for (var i=0; i<removeSouth2021.length; i++){
	    if (removeSouth2021[i].innerText === '2021 South'){
	       removeSouth2021[i].remove();
	    }
	}
}

// Change Midwest to Central on Main Parent Menu (nav-x82490):

var changemidwest = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82490 li > a');
if (changemidwest != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<changemidwest.length; i++){
        if (changemidwest[i].innerText === '2021 Midwest'){
          var node = changemidwest[i]
          node.innerText = node.innerText.replace("2021 Midwest", "2021 Central");
          node.href = node.href.replace("2021-midwest", "2021-central");
        }
    }
} 

// Change Midwest to Central on Submenu (nav-x82502):

var centralsub = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82502 li > a');
if (centralsub != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<centralsub.length; i++){
        if (centralsub[i].innerText === '2021 Midwest'){
          var node = centralsub[i]
          node.innerText = node.innerText.replace("2021 Midwest", "2021 Central");
          node.href = node.href.replace("2021-midwest", "2021-central");
        }
    }
} 

// Change East Regional to East on Main Parent Menu (nav-x82490):

var changeeast = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82490 li > a');
if (changeeast != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<changeeast.length; i++){
        if (changeeast[i].innerText === '2021 East Regional'){
          var node = changeeast[i]
          node.innerText = node.innerText.replace("2021 East Regional", "2021 East");
          node.href = node.href.replace("2021-east-regional", "2021-east");
        }
    }
} 

// Change East Regional to East on Submenu (nav-x82495):

var eastsub = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82495 li > a');
if (eastsub != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<eastsub.length; i++){
        if (eastsub[i].innerText === '2021 East Regional'){
          var node = eastsub[i]
          node.innerText = node.innerText.replace("2021 East Regional", "2021 East");
          node.href = node.href.replace("2021-east-regional", "2021-east");
        }
    }
} 

// Change Match Results on East submenu to Brackets:

var bracketseast = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82495 li > a');
if (bracketseast != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<bracketseast.length; i++){
        if (bracketseast[i].innerText === 'Match Results'){
          var node = bracketseast[i]
          node.innerText = node.innerText.replace("Match Results", "Brackets");
          node.href = node.href.replace("match-results", "brackets");
        }
    }
} 

// Change Match Results on Central submenu to Brackets:

var bracketscentral = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82502 li > a');
if (bracketscentral != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<bracketscentral.length; i++){
        if (bracketscentral[i].innerText === 'Match Results'){
          var node = bracketscentral[i]
          node.innerText = node.innerText.replace("Match Results", "Brackets");
          node.href = node.href.replace("match-results", "brackets");
          node.href = node.href.replace("2021-midwest", "2021-central");
        }
    }
} 


// Change Match Results on West submenu to Brackets:

var bracketswest = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82507 li > a');
if (bracketswest != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<bracketswest.length; i++){
        if (bracketswest[i].innerText === 'Match Results'){
          var node = bracketswest[i]
          node.innerText = node.innerText.replace("Match Results", "Brackets");
          node.href = node.href.replace("match-results", "brackets");
        }
    }
} 


// Update Central Teams link:

var bracketscentral = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82502 li > a');
if (bracketscentral != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<bracketscentral.length; i++){
        if (bracketscentral[i].innerText === 'Teams'){
          var node = bracketscentral[i]
          node.href = node.href.replace("2021-midwest", "2021-central");
        }
    }
} 

// Update Awards Teams link:

var bracketscentral = document.querySelectorAll('#nav-x82502 li > a');
if (bracketscentral != null){ 
    for (var i=0; i<bracketscentral.length; i++){
        if (bracketscentral[i].innerText === 'Awards'){
          var node = bracketscentral[i]
          node.href = node.href.replace("2021-midwest", "2021-central");
        }
    }
}

				<path d="M63.85 0A63.85 63.85 0 1 1 0 63.85 63.85 63.85 0 0 1 63.85 0zm.65 19.5a44 44 0 1 1-44 44 44 44 0 0 1 44-44z" fill="url(#linear-gradient)" fill-rule="evenodd"/>
				<animateTransform attributeName="transform" type="rotate" from="0 64 64" to="360 64 64" dur="1080ms" repeatCount="indefinite"></animateTransform>
				</g>
			</svg>
		</div>

		<div
			class="jet-mobile-menu__toggle-icon"
			v-if="!menuOpen && !toggleLoaderVisible"
			v-html="toggleClosedIcon"
		></div>
		<div
			class="jet-mobile-menu__toggle-icon"
			v-if="menuOpen && !toggleLoaderVisible"
			v-html="toggleOpenedIcon"
		></div>
		<span
			class="jet-mobile-menu__toggle-text"
			v-if="toggleText"
			v-html="toggleText"
		></span>

	</div>

	<transition name="cover-animation">
		<div
			class="jet-mobile-menu-cover"
			v-if="menuContainerVisible && coverVisible"
			v-on:click="closeMenu"
		></div>
	</transition>

	<transition :name="showAnimation">
		<div
			class="jet-mobile-menu__container"
			v-if="menuContainerVisible"
		>
			<div
				class="jet-mobile-menu__container-inner"
			>

					<div

					></div>
				</div>

					class="jet-mobile-menu__controls"
				>
					<div
						class="jet-mobile-menu__breadcrumbs"
						v-if="isBreadcrumbs"
					>
						<div

							v-for="(item, index) in breadcrumbsData"
							:key="index"
						>
							<div
								class="breadcrumb-label"

								v-html="item"
							></div>

					</div>
					<div
						class="jet-mobile-menu__back"
						ref="back"
						tabindex="1"

						v-if="!isBack && isClose"
						v-html="closeIcon"

						v-on:keyup.enter="menuToggle"
					></div>

					></div>
				</div>

					class="jet-mobile-menu__before-template"
					v-if="beforeTemplateVisible"
				>
					<div
						class="jet-mobile-menu__before-template-content"
						ref="before-template-content"
						v-html="beforeContent"
					></div>
				</div>

				<div
					class="jet-mobile-menu__body"
				>
					<transition :name="animation">
						<mobile-menu-list
							v-if="!templateVisible"
							:key="depth"

    <script type="text/javascript">
     //Header JS - Printing inline to prevent calling another asset

jQuery(function ($) {
    // Prevent closing from click inside dropdown
    $(document).on('click', '.dropdown-menu', function (e) {
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    <script type="text/javascript">
     jQuery(function ($){
  //change arrow direction on mobile
  $('.dropdown-toggle').on('click', function(){
        if ($(window).width() < 769) {
            if ($(this).hasClass('mbl-nav-open')){
                $(this).removeClass('mbl-nav-open');
                $('.nav-item.dropdown').show();
                $('.has-megamenu').removeClass('open');
		$('#outer_nav').removeClass('lock-mbl-menu');
            } else{
                $(this).addClass('mbl-nav-open');
                $('.nav-item.dropdown').hide();
                $(this).parent('.nav-item.dropdown').show();
		$('#outer_nav').addClass('lock-mbl-menu');
            }
        } else{
	    window.location.href = $(this).attr('href');
	}
  });

      $(window).scroll(function(){
        if ($(window).width() > 768) {
            var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
            if (scrollTop > 120) {
                $('#outer_nav').css('opacity','0');
                $('#outer_nav').addClass('header-sticky');
                $('.navbar-brand img').attr('src', 'https://storage.googleapis.com/gal-uploads/1/2020/02/GU-Buff-White-768x593.png');
                      
            } else {
                $('#outer_nav').css('opacity','1');
                $('#outer_nav').removeClass('header-sticky');  
                $('.navbar-brand img').attr('src', 'https://storage.googleapis.com/gal-uploads/1/elementor/thumbs/GU-p2dj3hm3n1wfli7mdysrvaw604ywfsijae14pnxqm8.png');
            }
        }
      });

  if ($(window).width() < 769) {
    $('.navbar-brand img').attr('src', 'https://storage.googleapis.com/gal-uploads/1/2020/02/GU-Buff-White-768x593.png');
    $('button.navbar-toggler').on('click',function(){
        $('.dropdown-toggle').removeClass('mbl-nav-open');
        if (document.querySelector('.sticky-links-tab').style.display === 'none') {
            document.querySelector('.sticky-links-tab').style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            document.querySelector('.sticky-links-tab').style.display = 'none';
        }
    });
  } 

  $(window).resize(function(){
    if ($(window).width() < 769) {
        $('.navbar-brand img').attr('src', 'https://storage.googleapis.com/gal-uploads/1/2020/02/GU-Buff-White-768x593.png');
        $('#outer_nav').css('opacity','1');
    } else {
        $('.navbar-brand img').attr('src', 'https://storage.googleapis.com/gal-uploads/1/elementor/thumbs/GU-p2dj3hm3n1wfli7mdysrvaw604ywfsijae14pnxqm8.png');
    }
  });

  $('#searchbox').on('keyup', function(e){
    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.keyCode === 13) {
        var currentSearchQuery = $('#searchbox').val();
        window.location.href = "https://www.gallaudet.edu/search-results?terms=" + currentSearchQuery;
    }
  });

});
    </script>
   </div>
  </nav>
